## Idea

The orbit of a point `x` for a permutation `f` is the set of point obtained by iterating `f` on `x`.

...

## Properties

### For type equipped with a counting, orbits of permutations are finite

<pre class="Agda"><a id="6061" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="6068" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6068" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="6072" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6073" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6073" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="6075" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6077" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="6082" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6084" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6085" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6085" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="6087" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6089" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#222" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="6092" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6073" class="Bound">l</a><a id="6093" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6095" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6096" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6096" class="Bound">eX</a> <a id="6099" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6101" href="univalent-combinatorics.counting.html#1746" class="Function">count</a> <a id="6107" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6085" class="Bound">X</a><a id="6108" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6110" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6111" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6111" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="6113" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6115" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6085" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="6117" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1607" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="6119" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6085" class="Bound">X</a><a id="6120" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6122" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6123" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6123" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="6125" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6127" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6085" class="Bound">X</a><a id="6128" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="6132" class="Keyword">where</a>
  
  <a id="6143" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6143" class="Function">two-points-iterate-Fin</a> <a id="6166" class="Symbol">:</a>
    <a id="6172" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#502" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="6174" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6175" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2072" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="6179" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6180" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1478" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="6187" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6188" href="univalent-combinatorics.counting.html#1874" class="Function">number-of-elements-count</a> <a id="6213" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6096" class="Bound">eX</a><a id="6215" class="Symbol">)))</a>
      <a id="6225" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="6227" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="6229" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6229" class="Bound">k1</a> <a id="6232" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6234" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#502" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="6236" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6237" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2072" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="6241" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6242" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1478" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="6249" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6250" href="univalent-combinatorics.counting.html#1874" class="Function">number-of-elements-count</a> <a id="6275" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6096" class="Bound">eX</a><a id="6277" class="Symbol">)))</a>
        <a id="6289" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="6291" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="6293" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6293" class="Bound">k2</a> <a id="6296" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6298" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6299" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#641" class="Datatype">Id</a> <a id="6302" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6303" <a id="6338" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6123" class="Bound">a</a><a id="6339" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6341" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6342" <a id="6377" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6123" class="Bound">a</a><a id="6378" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="6381" href="foundation-core.cartesian-product-types.html#577"   <a id="6400" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6143" class="Function">two-points-iterate-Fin</a> <a id="6423" class="Symbol">=</a>

  <a id="15177" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#15047" class="Function">mult-has-finite-orbits-permutation</a> <a id="15212" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1465" class="InductiveConstructor">zero-ℕ</a> <a id="15219" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="15221" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#694" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>

    <a id="15280" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="15282" href="elementary-number-theory.iterating-functions.html#874" class="Function">iterate-add-ℕ</a> <a id="15296" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15297" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers.html#1176" class="Function">mul-ℕ</a> <a id="15303" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#15271" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="15305" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15306" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#592" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="15310" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#13890" class="Function">has-finite-orbits-permutation</a><a id="15339" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="15342" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15343" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#592" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="15347" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#13890" class="Function">has-finite-orbits-permutation</a><a id="15376" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15378" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15379" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1807" class="Function">map-equiv</a> <a id="15389" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6111" class="Bound">f</a><a id="15390" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15392" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6123" class="Bound">a</a><a id="15393" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15395" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1239" class="Function Operator">∙</a>
      <a id="15403" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="15405" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2853" class="Function">ap</a> <a id="15408" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15409" href="elementary-number-theory.iterating-functions.html#566" class="Function">iterate</a> <a id="15417" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15418" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers.html#1176" class="Function">mul-ℕ</a> <a id="15424" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#15271" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="15426" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15427" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#592" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="15431" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#13890" class="Function">has-finite-orbits-permutation</a><a id="15460" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="15463" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15464" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1807" class="Function">map-equiv</a> <a id="15474" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6111" class="Bound">f</a><a id="15475" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="15478" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15479" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#604" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="15483" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15484" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#604" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="15488" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#13890" class="Function">has-finite-orbits-permutation</a><a id="15517" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="15520" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1239" class="Function Operator">∙</a>
        <a id="15530" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="15532" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#15047" class="Function">mult-has-finite-orbits-permutation</a> <a id="15567" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#15271" class="Bound">k</a><a id="15568" class="Symbol">))</a>
</pre>      
### For finite types, the number of orbits-permutation of a permutation is finite.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="15674" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="15681" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#15681" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="15685" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15686" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#15686" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="15688" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15690" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="15695" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15697" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15698" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#15698" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="15700" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15702" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1444" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="15703" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15705" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15706" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#15706" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="15708" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15710" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#4556" class="Function">UU-Fin-Level</a> <a id="15723" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#15686" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="15725" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#15698" class="Bound">n</a><a id="15726" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15728" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15729" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#15729" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="15731" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15733" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15734" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#4651" class="Function">type-UU-Fin-Level</a> <a id="15752" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#15706" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="15754" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1607" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="15756" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#4651" class="Function">type-UU-Fin-Level</a> <a id="15774" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#15706" class="Bound">X</a><a id="15775" class="Symbol">))</a>

                <a id="16425" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="16427" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2853" class="Function">ap</a> <a id="16430" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16431" href="elementary-number-theory.iterating-functions.html#566" class="Function">iterate</a> <a id="16439" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16440" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#592" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="16444" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16445" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#17009" class="Function">lemma</a> <a id="16451" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#16322" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="16453" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#16173" class="Bound">k</a><a id="16454" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="16457" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16458" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1807" class="Function">map-equiv</a> <a id="16468" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#15729" class="Bound">f</a><a id="16469" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="16472" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16473" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1552" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="16477" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#16175" class="Bound">p</a><a id="16478" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16480" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1239" class="Function Operator">∙</a>

    <a id="16748" class="Keyword">where</a>

                  <a id="20312" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="20314" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20315" href="elementary-number-theory.addition-natural-numbers.html#2076" class="Function">commutative-add-ℕ</a>

    <a id="69902" href="univalent-combinatorics.counting.html#1746" class="Function">count</a>

        <a id="78412" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2853" class="Function">ap</a> <a id="78415" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="78418" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#78418" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="78420" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="78422" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#7591" class="Function">succ-Fin</a> <a id="78431" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="78432" href="elementary-number-theory.iterating-functions.html#566" class="Function">iterate</a> <a id="78440" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="78441" href="elementary-number-theory.addition-natural-numbers.html#988" class="Function">add-ℕ</a> <a id="78447" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="78448" href="univalent-combinatorics.counting.html#1874" class="Function">number-of-elements-count</a> <a id="78473" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#23799" class="Bound">eX</a><a id="78475" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="78477" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#78418" class="Bound">k</a><a id="78478" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="78480" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#7591" class="Function">succ-Fin</a> <a id="78489" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#7006" class="Function">zero-Fin</a><a id="78497" class="Symbol">))</a>
          <a id="78510" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="78511" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#71003" class="Function">number-orbits-composition-transposition</a> <a id="78551" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#77590" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="78553" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#78233" class="Bound">P</a><a id="78554" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="78560" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#77783" class="Function">cases-opposite-sign-composition-transposition</a> <a id="78606" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="78607" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1262" class="InductiveConstructor">inr</a> <a id="78611" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#78611" class="Bound">NP</a><a id="78613" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="78615" class="Symbol">=</a>
      <a id="78623" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2853" class="Function">ap</a> <a id="78626" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="78629" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#78629" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="78631" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="78633" href="elementary-number-theory.iterating-functions.html#566" class="Function">iterate</a> <a id="78641" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="78642" href="elementary-number-theory.addition-natural-numbers.html#988" class="Function">add-ℕ</a> <a id="78648" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="78649" href="univalent-combinatorics.counting.html#1874" class="Function">number-of-elements-count</a> <a id="78674" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#23799" class="Bound">eX</a><a id="78676" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="78678" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#78629" class="Bound">k</a><a id="78679" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="78681" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#7591" class="Function">succ-Fin</a> <a id="78690" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#7006" class="Function">zero-Fin</a><a id="78698" class="Symbol">)</a>
        <a id="78708" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="78710" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#76310" class="Function">number-orbits-composition-transposition&#39;</a> <a id="78751" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#77590" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="78753" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#78611" class="Bound">NP</a><a id="78755" class="Symbol">)</a>
